\"text\": \"CSS style changes in Firefox trigger a complex chain of events flowing from the DOM through the layout engine to WebRender compositing. The process can be traced through several key stages:\\n\\n**Stage 1: Style Change Notification**\\nWhen a CSS style changes (e.g., via element.style or attribute modifications), Element::NotifyStyleStateChange() and Element::NotifyStateChange() in dom/base/Element.cpp trigger notifications. These call into RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent() in layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp, which posts a restyle event to the pres context.\\n\\n**Stage 2: Frame Style Recomputation**\\nThe RestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames() function in layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp is the core of style recomputation. It processes the nsStyleChangeList (defined in layout/style/nsStyleChangeList.cpp) which collects all frames affected by the style change along with their nsChangeHint values (from layout/style/nsChangeHint.h). The ServoStyleSet in layout/style/ServoStyleSet.cpp integrates with the Servo style engine to recalculate computed styles. For each frame with a new computed style, nsIFrame::DidSetComputedStyle() is called (layout/generic/nsIFrame.cpp), allowing frames to react to style changes.\\n\\n**Stage 3: Dirty Frame and Reflow Scheduling**\\nBased on the nsChangeHint values, PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow() in layout/base/PresShell.cpp schedules frames for reflow. The change hints (like nsChangeHint_NeedReflow, nsChangeHint_NeedDirtyReflow, nsChangeHint_RepaintFrame) determine the type of reflow needed. Frame dirty bits such as NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY and NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN (defined in layout/generic/nsFrameStateBits.h) are set to mark frames requiring reflow or repaint.\\n\\n**Stage 4: Display List Construction**\\nDuring the paint phase, nsDisplayListBuilder in layout/painting/nsDisplayList.cpp walks the frame tree and constructs a display list of painting instructions. Each frame's BuildDisplayList() method (in layout/generic/nsIFrame.cpp) is called to contribute display items. The nsDisplayList.h header defines the various nsDisplayItem types that represent visual elements to be rendered. InvalidateFrame() methods in nsIFrame.cpp mark regions as needing repainting.\\n\\n**Stage 5: WebRender Layer Update**\\nThe WebRenderLayerManager in gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderLayerManager.cpp receives the constructed display list and calls EndTransactionWithoutLayer(). The WebRenderCommandBuilder in gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderCommandBuilder.cpp transforms the display list into WebRender commands through CreateWebRenderCommandsFromDisplayList(). The RenderRootStateManager in gfx/layers/wr/RenderRootStateManager.cpp manages the WebRender backend state and resource updates. Finally, the WebRenderBridgeParent in gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderBridgeParent.cpp receives the display list data via SetDisplayList() and sends it to the WebRender compositor on the compositor thread for rendering.\\n\\nThis chain demonstrates how a single CSS style change propagates from DOM mutation through layout invalidation, frame reflow, display list construction, and finally to WebRender compositing for efficient multi-threaded rendering.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3490,"cache_read_input_tokens":109588,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3490},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"8d125413-a2ab-43cd-b608-29b1cb7da9bc","uuid":"a4b678e7-4708-4ae2-8346-577f5221e961"}
